				}

		}

			hidden_trigger = {
				tag = SOV
			}
			HUN = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
				NOT = {
					is_puppet_of = SOV
				}
			}
		}
		icon = GFX_SOV_influence_RUS
		available = {
			HUN = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = {
							has_completed_focus = SOV_reform_csto
						}
					}
					fascist > 0.25
				}
				else_if = {
					fascist > 0.4
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 0
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 25
		}
		remove_effect = {
			add_to_faction = HUN
			HUN = {
				clr_country_flag = global_ass_lol
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = SOV_holy_union_reborn } 
					set_country_flag = hu_member
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = SOV_reform_csto } 
					set_country_flag = esto_member
				}
			}
		}
	}
	SOV_puppet_hungary_ldpr = {
		visible = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				tag = SOV
			}
			HUN = {
				NOT = {
					is_puppet_of = SOV
				}
			}

				is_in_faction_with = SOV

		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 20
		cost = 75

				remove_ideas = SOV_unstable_government
				if = {
					limit = { SOV = { has_completed_focus = SOV_political_independency } }
					add_ideas = SOV_relaxed_political_control_idea
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { SOV = { has_completed_focus = SOV_export_national_democracy } }
					add_ideas = SOV_exported_national_democracy_idea
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { SOV = { has_completed_focus = SOV_centralized_armies } }
					add_ideas = SOV_unified_command_ldpr_idea
				}			
				if = {
					limit = { SOV = { has_completed_focus = SOV_russian_market_development } }
					add_ideas = SOV_united_economic_sphere_idea
				}			
				if = {
					limit = { SOV = { has_completed_focus = SOV_increase_direct_rule } }
					add_ideas = SOV_direct_rule_from_moscow_idea
				}	
				if = {
					limit = { SOV = { has_completed_focus = SOV_bulwark_against_decadency } }
					add_ideas = SOV_european_bulwark_idea
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascist
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = fascist
						popularity = 0.21
					}

	SOV_waning_coronavirus_mission = {
		icon = generic_coronavirus
		allowed = {
			tag = SOV
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea4
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea3
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea2
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea1
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SOV_vladimir_putin
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_flag = SOV_dealt_with_coronavirus
					has_country_flag = SOV_corona_decision
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		activation = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea4
				has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea3
				has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea2
				has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea1
				has_idea = SOV_coronavirus_pandemic_idea
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = SOV_vladimir_putin
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_flag = SOV_dealt_with_coronavirus
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 50
		timeout_effect = {
			SOV_decrease_corona = yes
			activate_mission = SOV_waning_coronavirus_mission
		}
		complete_effect = {
		}
	}
}
